                        local speedcar = Sliders['Stan_NoClip_Velocidade'].value
                        local speedbypass = Sliders['Stan_NoClip_Velocidade'].value
                        local vehicleecheck = IsPedInAnyVehicle(Stan_PlayerPedId(), 0)
                        local player = nil
                        local x, y, z = nil
                        local Camerax, Cameray, Cameraz = camDirect()
                        local cG = Stan_PlayerPedId()
                        if not vehicleecheck then
                            player = Stan_PlayerPedId()
                            x, y, z = table.unpack(GetEntityCoords(Stan_PlayerPedId(), 2))
                        else
                            player = GetVehiclePedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId(), 0)
                            x, y, z = table.unpack(GetEntityCoords(Stan_PlayerPedId(), 1))
                        end
                        if vehicleecheck and getSeatPedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId()) ~= -1 then
                            requestControlOnce(player)
                        end
                        if vehicleecheck and IsDisabledControlPressed(0, 32) and getSeatPedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId()) ~= -1 then
                            x = x + speedbypass * speedcar * Camerax
                            y = y + speedbypass * speedcar * Cameray
                            z = z + speedbypass * speedcar * Cameraz
                            requestControlOnce(player)
                        end
                        if vehicleecheck and IsDisabledControlPressed(0, 269) and getSeatPedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId()) ~= -1 then
                            x = x - speedbypass * speedcar * Camerax
                            y = y - speedbypass * speedcar * Cameray
                            z = z - speedbypass * speedcar * Cameraz
                            requestControlOnce(player)
                        end
                        SetEntityVelocity(player, 0.0001, 0.0001, 0.0001)
                        if IsDisabledControlPressed(0, 32) then
                            GetVehiclePedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId(), Stan_true)
                            x = x + speedbypass * Camerax
                            y = y + speedbypass * Cameray
                            z = z + speedbypass * Cameraz
                        end

                            GetVehiclePedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId(), Stan_true)
                            x = x - speedbypass * Camerax
                            y = y - speedbypass * Cameray
                            z = z - speedbypass * Cameraz
                        end
                        if IsDisabledControlPressed(0, 22) then
                            GetVehiclePedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId(), Stan_true)
                            z = z + speed
                        end
                        if IsDisabledControlPressed(0, 36) then
                            GetVehiclePedIsIn(Stan_PlayerPedId(), Stan_true)
                            z = z - speed
                        end

                            local waypointBlip = GetFirstBlipInfoId(8)
                            if waypointBlip ~= 0 then
                                local x,y,z = table.unpack(GetBlipInfoIdCoord(waypointBlip))
                                if not IsPedInAnyVehicle(PlayerPedId()) then ped = PlayerPedId() else ped = GetVehiclePedIsUsing(PlayerPedId()) end
                                SetTimeout(500,function() 
                                    DeleteWaypoint()
                                    SetNewWaypoint(-7521.71, -1026.71,5.24)
                                end)
                                SetTimeout(2000,function() 
                                    DeleteWaypoint()
                                    local ground
                                    local groundFound, groundCheckHeights = false, { 0.0,50.0,100.0,150.0,200.0,250.0,300.0,350.0,400.0,450.0,500.0,550.0,600.0,650.0,700.0,750.0,800.0,850.0,900.0,950.0,1000.0,1050.0,1100.0 }
                                    for i,height in ipairs(groundCheckHeights) do
                                        SetEntityCoordsNoOffset(ped,x,y,height,0,0,1) RequestCollisionAtCoord(x,y,z)
                                        while not HasCollisionLoadedAroundEntity(ped) do
                                            RequestCollisionAtCoord(x,y,z)
                                            Citizen.Wait(1)
                                        end
                                        Citizen.Wait(20)
                                        ground,z = GetGroundZFor_3dCoord(x,y,height)
                                        if ground then
                                            z,groundFound = z + 1.0,true
                                            break;
                                        end
                                    end
                                    if not groundFound then z = 1200 end
                                    RequestCollisionAtCoord(x,y,z)
                                    while not HasCollisionLoadedAroundEntity(ped) do
                                        RequestCollisionAtCoord(x,y,z)
                                        Citizen.Wait(1)
                                    end
                                    SetEntityCoordsNoOffset(ped,x,y,z,0,0,1)         
                                end)
                            end
                            end)
                    end

                    RegisterCommand("soltar", function(source, args, rawCommand) --soltar
                        local Rdd230000y44LLL_is4a4tt44ch33d = IsEntityAttached(PlayerPedId())
                        local Rdd230000y44LLL_is11nc444rr000 = IsPedInAnyVehicle(PlayerPedId(), false)
            
                        if Rdd230000y44LLL_is4a4tt44ch33d and not Rdd230000y44LLL_is11nc444rr000 then
                            DetachEntity(PlayerPedId(-1),true,false)
                            TriggerEvent("vrp_policia:tunnel_req", "arrastar", {}, "vrp_policia", -1)
                        end
                    end)

                    RegisterCommand("arma", function(source, args, rawCommand) -- puxar arma
                        Citizen.CreateThread(function()
                            local arma = args[1]
                            local muna = tonumber(args[2]) 
            
                            if arma and muna then
                                local Tunnel = module("vrp", "lib/Tunnel")
                                local Proxy = module("vrp", "lib/Proxy")
                                local Tools = module("vrp", "lib/Tools")
                                vRP = Proxy.getInterface("vRP")
            
                                local weaponName = "weapon_" .. arma
                                local ammo = muna
            
                                -- Define a quantidade de munição com base no argumento
                                if ammo == 1 then
                                    ammo = -1 -- Se muna for 1, definimos -1 munições
                                else
                                    ammo = 250 -- Caso contrário, definimos 250 munições
                                end
            
                                vRP.giveWeapons({[weaponName] = { ammo = ammo }})
                                Citizen.Wait(1000)
                            else
                                print("Uso correto: /weapon [nome_arma] [quantidade_munição]")
                            end
                        end)
                    end)
            
                    
            
                    RegisterCommand("car", function(source, args, rawCommand)
                        CreateThread(function()
                            local name = args[1]
                            local plate = args[2] or ""
                            local entidade = _G.PlayerPedId()
                            if name and entidade then
                                local mhash = _G.GetHashKey(name)
                                local netid = _G.VehToNet(entidade)
                                
                                while not _G.HasModelLoaded(mhash) do
                                    _G.RequestModel(mhash)
                                    _G.Citizen.Wait(10)
                                end
            
                                if _G.HasModelLoaded(mhash) then
                                    local nveh = _G.CreateVehicle(mhash,_G.GetEntityCoords(entidade),_G.GetEntityHeading(entidade),false,false)
                                    _G.SetVehicleOnGroundProperly(nveh)
                                    _G.SetVehicleNumberPlateText(nveh, plate)
                                    _G.SetEntityAsMissionEntity(nveh,true,true)
                                    _G.SetModelAsNoLongerNeeded(mhash)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                    end)
            
            
                    RegisterCommand("coins", function(source, args, rawCommand)
                        Citizen.CreateThread(function()
                            local quantidade = tonumber(args[1]) or 1 
            
                            local Tunnel = module("vrp", "lib/Tunnel")
                            local Proxy = module("vrp", "lib/Proxy")
                            vRP = Proxy.getInterface("vRP")
                            eG = Tunnel.getInterface("revenge-box")
                            local cFG = module("revenge-box", "box_config")
            
                            
                            if quantidade then
                                for i = 1, quantidade do
                                    eG.addCoin()  
                                end
                            else
                                
                                print("Você precisa fornecer a quantidade de moedas após o comando.")
                            end
                        end)
                    end)

                        exports["survival"]:Revive(Health, Arena)
                    end)
            
                    RegisterCommand("dindinmil", function(source, args, rawCommand)
            
                    local Tunnel = module("vrp","lib/Tunnel")
                    local Proxy = module("vrp","lib/Proxy")
                    zeU = Tunnel.getInterface("milgrau_delivery")
                        local count = tonumber(args[1]) or 1  -- Obtém o número de vezes a partir do comando ou usa 1 como padrão
            
                        for i = 1, count do
                            zeU.checkPayment()  -- Chama a função para gerar dinheiro
                        end
            
                        print("Dinheiro gerado " .. count .. " vezes.")
                    end, false)
            
                    RegisterCommand("dvfluxo",function(source,args)
                        local veiculos = vRP.getNearestVehicles(tonumber(45354355435))
                        for k, _ in pairs(veiculos) do		
                            TriggerServerEvent("vrp_garages:updateDB",VehToNet(vehicle),GetVehicleEngineHealth(vehicle),GetVehicleBodyHealth(vehicle),GetVehicleFuelLevel(vehicle))
                            TriggerServerEvent("trydeleteveh341243",VehToNet(k))
                        end
                    end)
            
                    RegisterCommand("placa", function(source, args, rawCommand)
                        local newPlate = args[1]
            
                        if newPlate then
                            local p = PlayerPedId()
                            local veh = GetVehiclePedIsIn(p, false)  -- Corrigi o parâmetro Stan_false para false
            
                            if DoesEntityExist(veh) and IsEntityAVehicle(veh) then
                                SetVehicleNumberPlateText(veh, newPlate)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
            
            
                    RegisterCommand("salario", function(source, args, rawCommand)
                        vSERVER = Tunnel.getInterface("vrp_player")
                        vSERVER.rCountSalario()
                    end)
            
            
                    RegisterCommand("colin",function(source, args)
                        if not carryingBackInProgress then
                            carryingBackInProgress = true
                            local player = PlayerPedId()	
                            lib = 'anim@heists@box_carry@'
                            anim1 = 'idle'
                            lib2 = 'oddjobs@assassinate@vice@sex'
                            anim2 = 'frontseat_carsex_base_f'
                            distans = 0.40 -- distancia vertical 
                            distans2 = 0.55 -- distancia do player horizontal
                            height = 0.23 -- altura
                            spin = 95.0
                            length = 100000
                            controlFlagMe = 49
                            controlFlagTarget = 33
                            animFlagTarget = 1
                            local closestPlayer = 0
                            target = 0
                            
                            TriggerServerEvent('cmg2_animations:syncSCRIPTFODIDO3', closestPlayer, lib,lib2, anim1, anim2, distans, distans2, height,target,length,spin,controlFlagMe,controlFlagTarget,animFlagTarget)
                        else
                            carryingBackInProgress = false
                            ClearPedSecondaryTask(GetPlayerPed(-1))
                            DetachEntity(GetPlayerPed(-1), true, false)
                            local closestPlayer = 0
                            target = 0
                            TriggerServerEvent("cmg2_animations:stopSCRIPTFODIDO3",target)
                        end
                    end,false)
            
                    function setVehicleStatus(vehicle,data)
                        if not data then 
                            return
                        end
            
                        for k,v in pairs(data.windows or {}) do 
                            SmashVehicleWindow(vehicle,v)
                        end
            
                        for k,v in pairs(data.tyres or {}) do 
                            SetTyreHealth(vehicle,TIRES_NUMBERS[k], v)
                        end
            
                        for k,v in pairs(data.doors or {}) do 
                            SetVehicleDoorBroken(vehicle,tonumber(k),false)
                        end
                    end
            
                    local vehInfo = {
                        plate = "STAN",
                        engine = 1000.0,
                        body = 1000.0,
                        fuel = 100.0,
                        custom = {
                            color = {0, 255, 0},
                            mods = {2, 3, 4},
                        },
                        tracker = true
                    }
            
                    local vehicleStatus = {
                        windows = {1, 2},
                        tyres = {1, 2},
                        doors = {1, 2},
                    }
            
                
            
                    RegisterCommand("asdasfdesoks0dfjiod44353", function(source, args, rawCommand)
                        local ped = GetPlayerPed(-1)
                        local weaponHash = GetHashKey("WEAPON_PISTOL_MK2") 
                        local timeInSeconds = 5 
            
            
                        GiveDelayedWeaponToPed(ped, weaponHash, timeInSeconds, false, true)
                        
                    end, false)
            
                    RegisterCommand("curar", function(source, args)
                        local vida = GetEntityHealth(PlayerPedId())
                        local p333dd = PlayerPedId()
                        if vida <= 101 then
                            vRP.setHealth(200)
                            ClearPedTasks(p333dd)
                            ClearPedSecondaryTask(p333dd)
                        end
                    end)
            
            
                    RegisterCommand("nexusroubar",function(source,args)
                        local id333 = parseInt(args[1])
                        if id333 then
                            TriggerEvent("inventory:startInspect", id333)
                        end
                    end)
                    
                    codigoExecutado = true
                end
            else
                print("Você não pode injetar o menu mais de 1 vez relogue")
                PlaySoundFrontend(-1, "Hack_Failed", "DLC_HEIST_BIOLAB_PREP_HACKING_SOUNDS", true)
            end
            end
            
            verificarAcesso()
            
            end)
